NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
K. Devipriya, aged 18 years old, who is mentally retarded, daughter of Mr. Karuppusamy, born on
25th November 1995, (25-11-1995) residing at Old No. 2/316, New No. 2/172, Ambedkar Street, Vinayaga Nagar,
Pozhichalur, Chennai-600 074, shall henceforth be known as K. PRIYA.

Chennai,
3rd February 2014.

P. KARUPPUSAMY.
(Father.)

ADOPTION CANCELLED
Notice is hereby given by RM. Kalyani, wife of (late) RM. Ramanathan that, Adoption of RM. Narayanan by them has
been cancelled.
We have adopted a boy Named A. Lakshmanan aged about 11 years son of RM. Ajithkumar, Karaikudi on
24-10-2012 and the same have been registered in Doc. No.: 7022/24-10-2012 in the Book No.: 97/IV/2012 at Ponnamaravathy
Sub-Registered office, so that we have changed his name as “RM. NARAYANAN” and Published in Gazette Book No.: 46,
Part VI-Section 4 dated 28-11-2012.
Due to Some Family Circumstances, we have cancelled the adoption on 31-01-2013 and legally registered in
Doc-No.: 530/29-1-2013 in the Book No.: 4/2013 at Ponnamaravathy Sub-Registered office dated 31-1-2013.
As My Husband Mr. RM. Ramanathan has deceased on 17-10-2013. I am hereby publishing the notice for references of
cancellation.
Hereby after we don’t have any relationship with the above said boy A. Lakshmanan, son of RM. Ajithkumar.
Henceforth he can be called in his old name A. LAKSHMANAN.

Chennai,
4th February 2014.

(Sd).................................................
Notice given by
RM. KALYANI.

Mohamed Aadil Ashfaqu alias Mohamed Adil Ashfaq age 21+years (male) Who is mentally retarded, son of
M. ASHFAQ RAHMAN born on 9th December 1991 residing at Old No. 43, New No. 20, Subedar Hussain Street,
Royapettah, Chennai-600 014, shall henceforth be known as MOHAMED AADIL ASHFAQ.

Chennai,
7th February 2014.

M. ASHFAQ RAHMAN.
(Father.)
